class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><strong><span>Important:</span></strong><span> Dont save PayPal as a payment method during purchase. For more information about securely saving payment methods and optimizing the buyer experience, see our </span><a rel="nofollow" href="/docs/checkout/standard/best-practices/" target="_blank"><span>Best practices guide</span></a><span>.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="availability" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="availability" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#availability" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#availability" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Availability</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h4 id="see-supported-countries" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#see-supported-countries" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#see-supported-countries" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->See Supported Countries</h4><span>

    </span><li><span>United States</span></li><span>
</span></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="know-before-you-code" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="know-before-you-code" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#know-before-you-code" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#know-before-you-code" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Know before you code</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>This integration requires a PayPal Developer account.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>This procedure modifies an existing </span><a href="https:/docs/checkout/standard/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>standard payments</span></a><span> or </span><a href="https:/docs/checkout/advanced/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>advanced credit and debit card payments</span></a><span> integration.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Your payments integration must have a </span><a href="https:/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>server-side capture call</span></a><span> or a </span><a href="https:/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>server-side authorization and capture call</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>To save payment methods, you must be able to uniquely identify payers. For example, payers create an account and log in to your site.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Complete the steps in </span><a href="https:/api/rest/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Get started</span></a><span> to get the following sandbox account information from the Developer Dashboard:</span><ul><span>
            </span><li><span>Your sandbox account login information</span></li><span>
            </span><li><span>Your access token</span></li><span>
        </span></ul><span>
    </span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><div class="openInCodeSpaces-div"><span>
    </span><p class="open-in-codespaces-module--open_in_codespace__header--1pnpf"><span>Get up and running in GitHub Codespaces</span></p><span>
    </span><p class="open-in-codespaces-module--open_in_codespace__text--2kyec"><span><span>GitHub Codespaces are cloud-based development environments where you can code and test your PayPal integrations. </span></span><a href="/api/rest/sandbox/codespaces/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Learn more</span></a></p><span>
    </span><button class="medium-open-in-codespaces" alt-text="Open In GitHub Codespaces" pa-marked="1"></button><span>
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="how-it-works" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="how-it-works" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#how-it-works" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#how-it-works" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->How it works</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>PayPal encrypts payment method information and stores it in a digital vault for that customer.</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
</span><li><span>The payer saves their payment method.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>For a first-time payer, PayPal creates a customer ID. Store this within your system for future use.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>When the customer returns to your website and is ready to check out, pass their PayPal-generated customer ID to the JavaScript SDK. The customer ID tells the JavaScript SDK to save or reuse a saved payment method.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>The payer completes a billing agreement.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>The JavaScript SDK populates the checkout page with each saved payment method. Each payment method appears as a one-click button next to other ways to pay.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><span>The checkout process is now shorter because it uses saved payment information.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="return-payer-experience" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="discoverySectionWrapper"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><h2 id="return-payer-experience" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#return-payer-experience" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#return-payer-experience" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Return payer experience</h2></div><div style="width:100%" class="discovery-section"><div class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-discoverySection__SD8-t" style="background-color:#fff"><div class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionContainer__hHVxt"><div data-testid="pp-sectionContent"><div data-testid="pp-sectionBlurb" class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionBlurb__nHd0q"><div data-testid="pp-blurb" class="Blurb-module_pp-blurb__lzocM"><h2></h2><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>The following is an example of what a payer sees after they save their PayPal Wallet on your site. Returning payers can select their saved payment method at checkout to pay faster.</span></p><p></p><span>
</span><p><span>The payer uses a credit card in their PayPal Wallet in the following example:</span></p></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="pp-sectionImage" class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionImage__BX-KD"><div class="ImageContainer-module_pp-imageContainer__awIei ImageContainer-module_backdrop__ML0hr"><img data-testid="pp-image" src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/save_paypal_sdk.png" alt="Return payer experience"/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="use-cases" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="use-cases" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#use-cases" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#use-cases" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Use cases</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Businesses save payment methods if they want customers to: </span></p><ul><li><span>Check out without re-entering a payment method</span></li><li><span>Pay after use, for example, ride-sharing and food delivery</span></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="check-eligibility" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="check-eligibility" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#check-eligibility" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#check-eligibility" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Check eligibility</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><undefined></undefined></p><ol><li><span>Go to </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com" class="dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>paypal.com</span></a><span> and sign in with your business account.</span></li><li><span>Go to </span><strong><span>Account Settings</span></strong><span> &gt; </span><strong><span>Payment Preferences</span></strong><span> &gt; </span><strong><span>Save PayPal and Venmo payment methods</span></strong><span>.</span></li><li><span>In the Save PayPal and Venmo payment methods section, select </span><strong><span>Get Started</span></strong><span>.</span></li><li><span>When you submit profile details, PayPal reviews your eligibility to save PayPal Wallets and Venmo accounts.</span></li><li><span>After PayPal reviews your eligibility, you'll see a status of </span><strong><span>Success</span></strong><span>, </span><strong><span>Need more information</span></strong><span>, or </span><strong><span>Denied</span></strong><span>.</span></li></ol><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="1.-set-up-sandbox-to-save-payment-methods" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="1-set-up-sandbox-to-save-payment-methods" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#1-set-up-sandbox-to-save-payment-methods" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-set-up-sandbox-to-save-payment-methods" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->1. Set up sandbox to save payment methods</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>Set up your sandbox and live business accounts to save payment methods:</span></p><ol><li><span>Log in to the Developer Dashboard.</span></li><li><span>Under </span><strong><span>REST API apps</span></strong><span>, select your app name.</span></li><li><span>Under </span><strong><span>Sandbox App Settings</span></strong><span> &gt; </span><strong><span>App Feature Options</span></strong><span>, check </span><strong><span>Accept payments</span></strong><span>.</span></li><li><span>Expand </span><strong><span>Advanced options</span></strong><span>. Confirm that </span><strong><span>Vault</span></strong><span> is selected.</span></li></ol><p></p><span>
</span><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>To go live, you'll need to be vetted for PayPal Wallet. You can start the vetting process from the Merchant Servicing Dashboard.</span></p><ul><li><span>Only your sandbox business account is enabled for vaulting payment methods. Your developer account remains unaffected.</span></li><li><span>You'll complete production onboarding when you're ready to go live.</span></li></ul><p></p><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><p><strong><span>Tip:</span></strong><span> When prompted for data such as a phone number for the sandbox business request, enter any number that fits the required format. Since this is a sandbox request, the data doesn't have to be factual.</span></p></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="2.-generate-user-id-token-for-payer" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="2-generate-user-id-token-for-payer" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#2-generate-user-id-token-for-payer" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-generate-user-id-token-for-payer" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->2. Generate user ID token for payer</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>The OAuth 2.0 API to retrieve an </span><a href="/api/rest/authentication/#curl" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class=""><span>access_token</span></code></a><span> has an additional parameter, </span><code class=""><span>response_type</span></code><span>, that can be set to </span><code class=""><span>id_token</span></code><span>. Include the </span><code class=""><span>id_token</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>access_token</span></code><span> in the response.</span></p><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row"     </span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;caret-color:rgb(30,32,33);color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:auto;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:auto;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(250,248,251);text-decoration:none"><span>
        </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Copy the sample request code.</span></li><span>
        </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Change</span><span class="Apple-converted-space"><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CLIENT_ID</span></code><span class="Apple-converted-space"><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to your client ID.</span></li><span>
        </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Change</span><span class="Apple-converted-space"><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CLIENT_SECRET</span></code><span class="Apple-converted-space"><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to your client secret.</span></li><span>

style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>A successful request returns fields including an </span><code class=""><span>access_token</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>id_token</span></code><span>, and the number of seconds the </span><code class=""><span>access_token</span></code><span> token is valid.</span></p><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>id_token</span></code><span>:</span></p><ul><li><span>Uniquely identifies each payer.</span></li><li><span>Expires in a few minutes because it's meant to be used during checkout. Generate new tokens if the current tokens expire.</span></li></ul><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><p><strong><span>Tip</span></strong><span>: Each buyer session is unique. </span><p><span>Pass the </span><code class=""><span>id_token</span></code><span> from your server into the JavaScript SDK using the </span><code class=""><span>data-user-id-token</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>

class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div><span>
    </span><h3 id="server-side-code-snippet" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#server-side-code-snippet" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#server-side-code-snippet" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-serversidecodesnippet" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-serversidecodesnippet" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Server-side code snippet</h3><span>
   
    </span><p><span>Set up your server to call the Create Order API. The button that the payer selects determines the </span><code class=""><span>payment_source</span></code><span> sent in the following sample.</span></p><span>
    </span><p><span>This SDK uses the Orders v2 API to save payment methods in the background. Use the following request to add attributes needed to save a PayPal Wallet.</span></p><span>
    </span><h4 id="request" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#request" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#request" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-request" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-request" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Request</h4><span>
    </span><p><span>In the following request, the </span><code class=""><span>payment_source.paypal.attributes.vault.store_in_vault</span></code><span> with the value </span><code class=""><span>ON_SUCCESS</span></code><span> means the PayPal button is saved with a successful authorization or capture.</span></p><span>
    </span><p><span>Pass the </span><code class=""><span>payment_source.paypal.experience_context</span></code><span> and include the </span><code class=""><span>return_url</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>cancel_url</span></code><span> to redirect the payer after they approve or cancel the order.</span></p><span>
    </span><p></p><span>
    </span><p><span>Create an order with PayPal as a payment source and store the PayPal Wallet in vault:</span></p><span>

Payer approval</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><span>
</span><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>If payer approval is required, the client SDK calls the payer approval flow. The approval flow takes the payer through PayPal Checkout.</span></p><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="7.-authorize-or-capture-order" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><h2 id="-7-authorize-or-capture-order" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#-7-authorize-or-capture-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#-7-authorize-or-capture-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> 7. data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3 id="capture-order-response" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#capture-order-response" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#capture-order-response" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-captureorderresponse" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-captureorderresponse" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Capture order response</h3><span>
</span><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>The HTTP response codes </span><code class=""><span>HTTP 2xx</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>HTTP 200</span></code><span> are returned for a successful request.</span></p><p><span>The capture is successful if the </span><code class=""><span>purchase_units[0].payments.captures.status</span></code><span> is </span><code class=""><span>COMPLETED</span></code><span>. You can confirm with the payer that the payment has been captured.</span></p><p><span>In the response from the authorize or capture request, the Orders v2 API interacts with the Payment Method Tokens v3 API. The Payment Method Tokens v3 API allows a PayPal Wallet to be saved. The response from the Orders v2 API contains the:</span></p><ul><li><code class=""><span>vault.id</span></code></li><li><code class=""><span>customer.id</span></code></li><li><code class=""><span>vault.status</span></code></li><li><code class=""><span>links</span></code><span> for the payment token of a recently saved PayPal Wallet.</span></li></ul><p></p><span>
</span><h4 id="capture-order" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#capture-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#capture-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-captureorder" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-captureorder" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Capture order</h4></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h4 id="save-approved-payment-source" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#save-approved-payment-source" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#save-approved-payment-source" href="#link-saveapprovedpaymentsource" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Save approved payment source</h4><span>
</span><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>If the payment has been authorized or captured, the payer does not need to be present to save a </span><code class=""><span>payment_source</span></code><span>. To keep checkout times as short as possible, the Orders API responds as soon as payment is captured.</span></p><p><span>If the </span><code class=""><span>attributes.vault.status</span></code><span> returned after payment is </span><code class=""><span>APPROVED</span></code><span>, you won't have a </span><code class=""><span>vault.id</span></code><span> yet. API still saves the payment source even after the Orders API returns its response and sends a webhook after the payment source is saved.</span></p><p><span>In order to retrieve a </span><code class=""><span>vault_id</span></code><span> when an </span><code class=""><span>APPROVED</span></code><span> status is returned, you'll need to subscribe to the </span><code class=""><span>VAULT.PAYMENT-TOKEN.CREATED</span></code><span> </span><a href="/api/rest/webhooks/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>webhook</span></a><span>.</span></p><p><span>The Payment Method Tokens API sends a webhook after the payment source is saved. An example of the </span><code class=""><span>VAULT.PAYMENT-TOKEN.CREATED</span></code><span> webhook payload is shown in the following sample:</span></p><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div Test your integration</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><undefined></undefined></p><p><span>Run the following tests in the PayPal sandbox to ensure you can save PayPal Wallets.</span></p><h3 id="save-payment-method" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#save-payment-method" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#save-payment-method" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-savepaymentmethod" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-savepaymentmethod" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Save payment method</h3><ol><li><span>On your checkout page, click the  PayPal button.</span></li><li><span>Log in to the payer account and approve the payment and billing agreement.</span></li><li><span>Capture the transaction.</span></li><li><span>Store the PayPal-generated customer ID in your system.</span></li><li><span>Log in to </span><a href="https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/" class="dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>sandbox</span></a><span> with your merchant account and verify the transaction.</span></li><li><span>Refresh the page that contains the  PayPal button. Ensure the JavaScript SDK is initialized with the PayPal-generated customer ID.</span></li><li><span>Ensure the  PayPal button displays the payer's preferred payment method.</span></li><li><span>Ensure that the payment method you just saved is visible with the other buttons.</span></li><li><span>Select the  PayPal button again to test the return payer flow.</span></li></ol><p></p><span>
</span><h3 id="sample-integration" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#sample-integration" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#sample-integration" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-sampleintegration" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-sampleintegration" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Sample integration</h3><span>

Wallet with JavaScript SDK | PayPal Developer","description":"Enable faster checkout by saving PayPal Wallets using the JavaScript SDK. Customers can manage transactions, funding sources, and recurring payments seamlessly."},"language":["en-US"],"ecm":{"link":"https://internal.paypalinc.com/contentmanager/space/b7241346-cd3d-4e70-a1c7-74bfd4aaab3d/environment/ddea4eb4-f0c4-4321-aa67-654e40fe9a18/entries/01rOKAtUrWUUWeXMZ4TWKx","envAllowsPreview":true},"markdownContent":"---\ntitle: Save PayPal with the JavaScript SDK\nslug: /docs/checkout/save-payment-methods/during-purchase/js-sdk/paypal/\ncreateTime: '2024-10-28T05:20:54.663Z'\nupdateTime: '2025-08-25T11:29:32.706Z'\n---\n\n\n# Save PayPal with the JavaScript SDK\n\n\n\nAfter customers save their PayPal Wallet, they can select it for faster checkout. Customers won't have to enter payment details for future transactions.\n\n\n\nTo save PayPal Wallets, payers need to log in to your site, make a purchase, and remain on your site when transactions take place.\n\n\n\nCustomers with a PayPal Wallet can:\n\n- Review PayPal transactions and transaction history\n- Review, add, or remove funding sources\n- Review and cancel recurring payments\n- Hold a balance in their PayPal account\n- Use PayPal to send and receive money\n- Withdraw money to a linked bank account\n- Use PayPal to transact with merchants\n\n\n\n\n**warning**\n**Important:** Dont save PayPal as a payment method during purchase. For more information about securely saving payment methods and optimizing the buyer experience, see our [Best practices guide](/docs/checkout/standard/best-practices/) .\n\n\n\n## Availability \n#### See Supported Countries\n- Australia\n- Austria\n- Belgium\n- Bulgaria\n- Canada\n- China\n- Cyprus\n- Czech Republic\n- Denmark\n- Estonia\n- Finland\n- France\n- Germany\n- Hong Kong\n- Hungary\n- Ireland\n- Italy\n- Japan\n- Latvia\n- Liechtenstein\n- Lithuania\n- Luxembourg\n- Malta\n- Netherlands\n- Norway\n- Poland\n- Portugal\n- Romania\n- Singapore\n- Slovakia\n- Slovenia\n- Spain\n- Sweden\n- United Kingdom\n- United States\n\n\n\n## Know before you code \n- This integration requires a PayPal Developer account.\n- This procedure modifies an existing [standard payments](https:/docs/checkout/standard/) or [advanced credit and debit card payments](https:/docs/checkout/advanced/) integration.\n- Your payments integration must have a [server-side capture call](https:/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture) or a [server-side authorization and capture call](https:/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture) .\n- To save payment methods, you must be able to uniquely identify payers. For example, payers create an account and log in to your site.\n- Complete the steps in [Get started](https:/api/rest/) to get the following sandbox account information from the Developer Dashboard: - Your sandbox account login information\n- Your access token\n\n \n\nGet up and running in GitHub Codespaces\n\nGitHub Codespaces are cloud-based development environments where you can code and test your PayPal integrations. [Learn more](/api/rest/sandbox/codespaces/)\n\n\n\n## How it works \nPayPal encrypts payment method information and stores it in a digital vault for that customer.\n\n- The payer saves their payment method.\n- For a first-time payer, PayPal creates a customer ID. Store this within your system for future use.\n- When the customer returns to your website and is ready to check out, pass their PayPal-generated customer ID to the JavaScript SDK. The customer ID tells the JavaScript SDK to save or reuse a saved payment method.\n- The payer completes a billing agreement.\n- The JavaScript SDK populates the checkout page with each saved payment method. Each payment method appears as a one-click button next to other ways to pay.\n\nThe checkout process is now shorter because it uses saved payment information.\n\n\n\n## Return payer experience \n\n\nThe following is an example of what a payer sees after they save their PayPal Wallet on your site. Returning payers can select their saved payment method at checkout to pay faster.\n\n\n\nThe payer uses a credit card in their PayPal Wallet in the following example:\n\n\n![Save Paypal SDK](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/save_paypal_sdk.png)\n\n\n## Use cases \nBusinesses save payment methods if they want customers to:\n\n- Check out without re-entering a payment method\n- Pay after use, for example, ride-sharing and food delivery\n\n\n\n## Check eligibility \n\n\n- Go to [paypal.com](https://www.paypal.com) and sign in with your business account.\n- Go to **Account Settings** \u0026gt; **Payment Preferences** \u0026gt; **Save PayPal and Venmo payment methods** .\n- In the Save PayPal and Venmo payment methods section, select **Get Started** .\n- When you submit profile details, PayPal reviews your eligibility to save PayPal Wallets and Venmo accounts.\n- After PayPal reviews your eligibility, you'll see a status of **Success** , **Need more information** , or **Denied** .\n\n\n\n\n\n## 1. Set up sandbox to save payment methods \n\n\nSet up your sandbox and live business accounts to save payment methods:\n\n- Log in to the Developer Dashboard.\n- Under **REST API apps** , select your app name.\n- Under **Sandbox App Settings** \u0026gt; **App Feature Options** , check **Accept payments** .\n- Expand **Advanced options** . Confirm that **Vault** is selected.\n\n\n\n\n\nTo go live, you'll need to be vetted for PayPal Wallet. You can start the vetting process from the Merchant Servicing Dashboard.\n\n- Only your sandbox business account is enabled for vaulting payment methods. Your developer account remains unaffected.\n- You'll complete production onboarding when you're ready to go live.\n\n\n\n**Tip:** When prompted for data such as a phone number for the sandbox business request, enter any number that fits the required format. Since this is a sandbox request, the data doesn't have to be factual.\n\n\n\n## 2. Generate user ID token for payer \n\n\nThe OAuth 2.0 API to retrieve an [access_token](/api/rest/authentication/#curl) has an additional parameter, response_type , that can be set to id_token . Include the id_token and access_token in the response.\n\n\n\n\n### First-time payer\nA payer wants to save a payment method for the first time. Modify the following code to generate a user ID token for the payer:\n\n### Sample server-side user ID token request\n \n\n1curl-s -X POST\"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token\"\\2-u CLIENT_ID:CLIENT_SECRET\\3-H\"Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded\"\\4-d\"grant_type=client_credentials\"\\5-d\"response_type=id_token\"### Modify the code\n- Copy the sample request code.\n- Change  CLIENT_ID  to your client ID.\n- Change  CLIENT_SECRET  to your client secret.\n\n\n,### Returning payer\nA payer wants to use a saved payment method. Use the saved PayPal-generated customer ID in the POST body parameter target_customer_id . The target_customer_id is:\n\n- a unique ID for a customer generated when the  payment_source  is saved to the vault\n- available when capturing the order or retrieving saved payment information.\n\n**Note:**  Use the customer identifier generated by PayPal and not the identifier that you use to identify the customer in your system.\n\n### Sample server-side user ID token request with a customer ID\n1curl-s -X POST\"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token\"\\2-u CLIENT_ID:CLIENT_SECRET\\3-H\"Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded\"\\4-d\"grant_type=client_credentials\"\\5-d\"response_type=id_token\"\\6-d\"target_customer_id=CUSTOMER-ID\"### Modify the code\n- Copy the sample request code.\n- Change  CLIENT_ID  to your client ID.\n- Change  CLIENT_SECRET  to your client secret.\n- Replace the PayPal-generated  CUSTOMER_ID  with the ID that was stored in your system.\n\n\n\n### Sample Response\n\n#### **`Code`**\n```javascript\n\n   {\n     \"access_token\" : \"A21AAJ--LVQmYlaxd_TDFOqVs4C3Xa7kPfa0Es7O35_9TEWaWRCMw7-NBJuBWqXZhb3eOolNnMtxwhoMP3NqHOJm1rvPDehfQ\",\n     \"app_id\" : \"APP-80W284485P519543T\",\n     \"expires_in\" : 32400,\n     \"id_token\" : \"eyJraWQiOiJjMmVjMmZiYjIzMGU0ZDkzOTNhMGFmZjEzZTY4MjFjMSIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCIsImFsZyI6IkVTMjU2In0.eyJpc3MiOiJodHRwczovL2FwaS5zYW5kYm94LnBheXBhbC5jb20iLCJzdWIiOiJQQ0haQ1RMMjVSNllXIiwiYWNyIjpbImNsaWVudCJdLCJzY29wZSI6WyJCcmFpbnRyZWU6VmF1bHQiXSwib3B0aW9ucyI6eyJjdXN0b21lcl9pZCI6IjIxMzM3NTk5MiJ9LCJheiI6ImdjcC5zbGMiLCJleHRlcm5hbF9pZCI6WyJQYXlQYWw6UENIWkNUTDI1UjZZVyIsIkJyYWludHJlZTo2ZDNtY3pqN2h3cHE4Y2cyIl0sImV4cCI6MTY2NDIzOTA1MCwiaWF0IjoxNjY0MjM4MTUwLCJqdGkiOiJVMkFBSVNTRkozbVlJUE8wdGYwTF93NFVmTHpfeGFCNHhYRndkTnRibTNXOVhtQ2xoU2NuWGZtMmRxbjU5QjY2akRVbzNhd1Y0ODlsbFpZOVBuV2RFTVN4ZlpZVDZKTS1mUi1rdEotcV9pdkZKMHlCWXdpdU1HaldPR2psZWktUSJ9.PSDUMcZxsEEUlKNqKHgFhrmAcKeCeJMIMhzMrVV5PpTftlB_Xmgzwl1Fir0H0OYSjmopcVPNfXyXl55jxaqJdQ\",\n     \"nonce\" : \"2022-09-27T00:22:30ZxsLQJVSYoAx7jqj1JJgr3onjVSPVL5juzZbId-Z-bwQ\",\n     \"scope\" : \"https://uri.paypal.com/services/invoicing https://uri.paypal.com/services/vault/payment-tokens/read https://uri.paypal.com/services/disputes/read-buyer https://uri.paypal.com/services/payments/realtimepayment https://uri.paypal.com/services/disputes/update-seller https://uri.paypal.com/services/paypalhere openid https://uri.paypal.com/services/payments/payment/authcapture https://uri.paypal.com/services/disputes/read-seller Braintree:Vault https://uri.paypal.com/services/payments/refund https://uri.paypal.com/services/identity/activities https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/vault/credit-card https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/payments/.* https://uri.paypal.com/services/reporting/search/read https://uri.paypal.com/payments/payouts https://uri.paypal.com/services/vault/payment-tokens/readwrite https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/vault/credit-card/.* https://uri.paypal.com/services/shipping/trackers/readwrite https://uri.paypal.com/services/subscriptions https://uri.paypal.com/services/applications/webhooks https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/payments/refund https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/payments/sale/.*/refund\",\n     \"token_type\" : \"Bearer\"\n  }\n \n```\n\n\nA successful request returns fields including an access_token , id_token , and the number of seconds the access_token token is valid.\n\nThe id_token :\n\n- Uniquely identifies each payer.\n- Expires in a few minutes because it's meant to be used during checkout. Generate new tokens if the current tokens expire.\n\n**Tip** : Each buyer session is unique. Set up your server to generate a new client token each time payment fields render on your page.\n\n\n\n\nPass the id_token from your server into the JavaScript SDK using the data-user-id-token .\n\n\n\n\n#### **`Code`**\n```curl\n\n  \u003cscript src=\"https://www.paypal.com/sdk/js?client-id=YOUR_CLIENT_ID\" data-user-id-token=\"YOUR-ID-TOKEN\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e\n\n```\n\n\n\n- Add the JavaScript SDK code to show the PayPal button on your product and checkout pages.\n- Determine where the SDK should show the PayPal button. Use [configuration attributes](/sdk/js/reference/#buttons) to control the layout of the button.\n\nHTML\n\n\n#### **`Code`**\n```javascript\n\n\u003c!-- Set up a container element for the button --\u003e\n\u003cdiv id=\"paypal-button-container\"\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c!-- Include the PayPal JavaScript SDK. Replace \u003cYOUR_CLIENT_ID\u003e with your client ID.--\u003e\n\u003cscript src=\"https://www.paypal.com/sdk/js?client-id=YOUR_CLIENT_ID\" data-user-id-token=\"YOUR-ID-TOKEN\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  // Render the eligible PayPal buttons within the #paypal-button-container\n  paypal.Buttons().render('#paypal-button-container')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n```\n\n\n\nInclude client-side callbacks to:\n\n- Manage interactions with APIs\n- Manage payer approval flows\n- Handle any events that lead to cancellation or error during payer approval\n\n\n\n### Client-side code snippet\n\n#### **`Code`**\n```javascript\n\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  paypal.Buttons({\n      // Call your server to set up the transaction\n      createOrder: function(data, actions) {\n        return fetch('/yourserver.com/createOrder', {\n          method: 'post',\n          body: JSON.stringify({\n            source: data.paymentSource, //paypal / venmo / etc.\n          }),\n          // Here for product info\n        }).then(function(res) {\n          return res.json();\n        }).then(function(orderData) {\n          return orderData.id;\n        });\n      },\n      // Authorize or capture the transaction after payer approves\n      onApprove: (data, actions) =\u003e {\n        return fetch('/yourserver.com/order/' + data.orderID + '/capture/', {\n          method: 'post'\n        });\n      },\n      onCancel(data, actions) {\n        console.log(`Order Canceled - ID: ${data.orderID}`);\n      },\n      onError(err) {\n        console.error(err);\n      }\n  }).render('#paypal-button-container');\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Server-side code snippet\nSet up your server to call the Create Order API. The button that the payer selects determines the payment_source sent in the following sample.\n\nThis SDK uses the Orders v2 API to save payment methods in the background. Use the following request to add attributes needed to save a PayPal Wallet.\n\n#### Request\nIn the following request, the payment_source.paypal.attributes.vault.store_in_vault with the value ON_SUCCESS means the PayPal button is saved with a successful authorization or capture.\n\nPass the payment_source.paypal.experience_context and include the return_url and cancel_url to redirect the payer after they approve or cancel the order.\n\n\n\nCreate an order with PayPal as a payment source and store the PayPal Wallet in vault:\n\n\n#### **`Code`**\n```javascript\n\n  curl -v -X POST https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ \\\n -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n -H \"Authorization: Bearer ACCESS-TOKEN\" \\\n -H \"PayPal-Request-Id: REQUEST-ID\" \\\n -d '{\n    \"intent\": \"CAPTURE\",\n    \"purchase_units\": [{\n      \"amount\": {\n        \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n        \"value\": \"100.00\"\n      }\n    }],\n    \"payment_source\": {\n      \"paypal\": {\n        \"attributes\": {\n          \"vault\": {\n            \"store_in_vault\": \"ON_SUCCESS\",\n            \"usage_type\": \"MERCHANT\",\n            \"customer_type\": \"CONSUMER\"\n          }\n        },\n      }\n    }\n  }'\n\n```\n\n#### Response\n\n\nReturn the id to your client to call the payer approval flow if the payment_source needs payer approval.\n\n**Note:** The request to save the PayPal button is made when the order is created through payment_source.attributes.vault.store_in_vault . Vault details are available only after an order is authorized or captured.\n\n\n\n\n#### **`code`**\n```javascript\n\n  {\n    \"id\": \"5O190127TN364715T\",\n    \"status\": \"PAYER_ACTION_REQUIRED\",\n    \"payment_source\": {\n      \"paypal\": {}\n    },\n    \"links\": [{\n        \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/5O190127TN364715T\",\n        \"rel\": \"self\",\n        \"method\": \"GET\"\n      },\n      {\n        \"href\": \"https://www.paypal.com/checkoutnow?token=5O190127TN364715T\",\n        \"rel\": \"payer-action\",\n        \"method\": \"GET\"\n      }\n    ]\n  }\n\n```\n\n\n## 6. Payer approval \n\n\nIf payer approval is required, the client SDK calls the payer approval flow. The approval flow takes the payer through PayPal Checkout.\n\n\n\n\n### \n### After the payer approves, the\u0026nbsp;onApprove\u0026nbsp;function is called in the JavaScript SDK. Depending on the intent passed, the server calls the following APIs:Capture Order API if the\u0026nbsp;intent\u0026nbsp;passed was\u0026nbsp;CAPTUREAuthorize Order API if the\u0026nbsp;intent\u0026nbsp;passed was\u0026nbsp;AUTHORIZE\u0026nbsp;as part of your Create Order call.If authorization or capture is successful, a\u0026nbsp;vault.id\u0026nbsp;is also created.Authorize order request\n\n#### **`code`**\n```javascript\n\n    curl -v -X POST https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/5O190127TN364715T/authorize \\\n -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n -H \"Authorization: Bearer ACCESS-TOKEN\" \\\n -d '{}'\n\n```\n\n#### Capture order request\n\n#### **`Capture order request`**\n```curl\ncurl -v -X POST https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/5O190127TN364715T/capture \\\n -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n -H \"Authorization: Bearer ACCESS-TOKEN\" \\\n -d '{}'\n\n```\n\n### Capture order response\n\n\nThe HTTP response codes HTTP 2xx or HTTP 200 are returned for a successful request.\n\nThe capture is successful if the purchase_units[0].payments.captures.status is COMPLETED . You can confirm with the payer that the payment has been captured.\n\nIn the response from the authorize or capture request, the Orders v2 API interacts with the Payment Method Tokens v3 API. The Payment Method Tokens v3 API allows a PayPal Wallet to be saved. The response from the Orders v2 API contains the:\n\n- vault.id\n- customer.id\n- vault.status\n- links for the payment token of a recently saved PayPal Wallet.\n\n\n\n#### Capture order\n\n#### **`code`**\n```javascript\n\n  {\n   \"id\": \"5O190127TN364715T\",\n   \"status\": \"COMPLETED\",\n   \"payment_source\": {\n     \"paypal\": {\n       \"attribute\": {\n         \"vault\": {\n           \"id\": \"3nqvjt3n\",\n           \"customer\": {\n               \"id\": \"208743798\"\n           },\n           \"status\": \"VAULTED\",\n           \"links\": [{\n               \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v3/vault/payment-tokens/3nqvjt3n\",\n               \"rel\": \"self\",\n               \"method\": \"GET\"\n             },\n             {\n               \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v3/vault/payment-tokens/3nqvjt3n\",\n               \"rel\": \"delete\",\n               \"method\": \"DELETE\"\n             },\n             {\n               \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/5O190127TN364715T\",\n               \"rel\": \"up\",\n               \"method\": \"GET\"\n             }\n           ]\n         }\n       },\n       \"name\": {\n         \"given_name\": \"Firstname\",\n         \"surname\": \"Lastname\"\n       },\n       \"email_address\": \"customer@example.com\",\n       \"phone_number\": {\n         \"national_number\": \"2025212022\"\n       },\n       \"account_id\": \"QYR5Z8XDVJNXQ\",\n       \"address\": {\n         \"country_code\": \"US\"\n       },\n     }\n   },\n   \"payer\": {\n     \"name\": {\n       \"given_name\": \"Firstname\",\n       \"surname\": \"Lastname\"\n     },\n     \"email_address\": \"customer@example.com\",\n     \"phone_number\": {\n       \"national_number\": \"2025212022\"\n     },\n     \"payer_id\": \"QYR5Z8XDVJNXQ\",\n     \"address\": {\n       \"country_code\": \"US\"\n     }\n   }\n   \"purchase_units\": [{\n     \"reference_id\": \"d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b\",\n     \"payments\": {\n       \"captures\": [{\n         \"id\": \"3C679366HH908993F\",\n         \"status\": \"COMPLETED\",\n         \"amount\": {\n           \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n           \"value\": \"100.00\"\n         },\n         \"seller_protection\": {\n           \"status\": \"ELIGIBLE\",\n           \"dispute_categories\": [\n             \"ITEM_NOT_RECEIVED\",\n             \"UNAUTHORIZED_TRANSACTION\"\n           ]\n         },\n         \"final_capture\": true,\n         \"seller_receivable_breakdown\": {\n           \"gross_amount\": {\n             \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n             \"value\": \"100.00\"\n           },\n           \"paypal_fee\": {\n             \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n             \"value\": \"3.00\"\n           },\n           \"net_amount\": {\n             \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n             \"value\": \"97.00\"\n           }\n         },\n         \"create_time\": \"2022-01-01T21:20:49Z\",\n         \"update_time\": \"2022-01-01T21:20:49Z\",\n         \"links\": [{\n             \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/payments/captures/3C679366HH908993F\",\n             \"rel\": \"self\",\n             \"method\": \"GET\"\n           },\n           {\n             \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/payments/captures/3C679366HH908993F/refund\",\n             \"rel\": \"refund\",\n             \"method\": \"POST\"\n           }\n         ]\n       }]\n     }\n   }],\n   \"links\": [{\n     \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/5O190127TN364715T\",\n     \"rel\": \"self\",\n     \"method\": \"GET\"\n   }]\n }\n\n```\n\n#### Save approved payment source\n\n\nIf the payment has been authorized or captured, the payer does not need to be present to save a payment_source . To keep checkout times as short as possible, the Orders API responds as soon as payment is captured.\n\nIf the attributes.vault.status returned after payment is APPROVED , you won't have a vault.id yet. An example of the attributes object from this scenario is in the following sample:\n\n\n\n\n#### **`code`**\n```javascript\n\n      \"attributes\": {\n        \"vault\": {\n          \"status\": \"APPROVED\",\n          \"links\": [\n            {\n              \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/5O190127TN364715T\",\n              \"rel\": \"up\",\n              \"method\": \"GET\"\n            }\n          ]\n        }\n      }\n\n```\n\n\nThe Payment Method Tokens API still saves the payment source even after the Orders API returns its response and sends a webhook after the payment source is saved.\n\nIn order to retrieve a vault_id when an APPROVED status is returned, you'll need to subscribe to the VAULT.PAYMENT-TOKEN.CREATED  [webhook](/api/rest/webhooks/) .\n\nThe Payment Method Tokens API sends a webhook after the payment source is saved. An example of the VAULT.PAYMENT-TOKEN.CREATED webhook payload is shown in the following sample:\n\n\n\n\n\n#### **`code`**\n```javascript\n\n       {\n  \"id\": \"WH-72S4353495632143A-68K769747M133873M\",\n  \"event_version\": \"1.0\",\n  \"create_time\": \"2022-08-27T01:25:57.462Z\",\n  \"resource_type\": \"payment_token\",\n  \"resource_version\": \"3.0\",\n  \"event_type\": \"VAULT.PAYMENT-TOKEN.CREATED\",\n  \"summary\": \"A payment token has been created.\",\n  \"resource\": {\n    \"time_created\": \"2022-08-26T18:25:57.449PDT\",\n    \"links\": [\n      {\n        \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v3/vault/payment-tokens/7vrxmrw\",\n        \"rel\": \"self\",\n        \"method\": \"GET\",\n        \"encType\": \"application/json\"\n      },\n      {\n        \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v3/vault/payment-tokens/7vrxmrw\",\n        \"rel\": \"delete\",\n        \"method\": \"DELETE\",\n        \"encType\": \"application/json\"\n      }\n    ],\n    \"id\": \"3nqvjt3n\",\n    \"payment_source\": {\n      \"paypal\": {\n        \"permit_multiple_payment_tokens\": false,\n        \"usage_type\": \"MERCHANT\",\n        \"customer_type\": \"CONSUMER\",\n        \"email_address\": \"email@example.com\",\n        \"payer_id\": \"VTR4JYK7STE7J\"\n      }\n    },\n    \"customer\": {\n      \"id\": \"208743798\"\n    }\n  },\n  \"links\": [\n    {\n      \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/notifications/webhooks-events/WH-72S4353495632143A-68K769747M133873M\",\n      \"rel\": \"self\",\n      \"method\": \"GET\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"href\": \"https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v1/notifications/webhooks-events/WH-72S4353495632143A-68K769747M133873M/resend\",\n      \"rel\": \"resend\",\n      \"method\": \"POST\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n \n```\n\n\nIn the previous example, the resource.id field is the vault ID. The resource.customer.id is the PayPal-generated customer ID.\n\n\n\n\n\n## 8. Test your integration \n\n\nRun the following tests in the PayPal sandbox to ensure you can save PayPal Wallets.\n\n### Save payment method\n- On your checkout page, click the  PayPal button.\n- Log in to the payer account and approve the payment and billing agreement.\n- Capture the transaction.\n- Store the PayPal-generated customer ID in your system.\n- Log in to [sandbox](https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/) with your merchant account and verify the transaction.\n- Refresh the page that contains the  PayPal button. Ensure the JavaScript SDK is initialized with the PayPal-generated customer ID.\n- Ensure the  PayPal button displays the payer's preferred payment method.\n- Ensure that the payment method you just saved is visible with the other buttons.\n- Select the  PayPal button again to test the return payer flow.\n\n\n\n### Sample integration\nSee a sample Save Payment Method integration in the [PayPal GitHub repository](https://github.com/paypal-examples/docs-examples/tree/main/save-payment-method) .\n\n\n\n## Next steps \n\n\n- [Test and go live](/reference/production/) with this integration.\n- Change the credentials and API URLs from api-m.sandbox.paypal.com to api-m.paypal.com when going live with your integration.\n- You can [create orders](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_create) without the payment_source.paypal.attributes.vault for subsequent or recurring transactions.\n- You can [get a payment token](/docs/api/payment-tokens/v3/#payment-tokens_get) , [list all payment tokens](/docs/api/payment-tokens/v3/#payment-tokens_payment-tokens) , [delete a payment token](/docs/api/payment-tokens/v3/#payment-tokens_delete) , and more with the Payment Method Tokens API.\n\n\n\n\n\n## See also \n- [Set up payment buttons](https:/docs/checkout/standard/)\n\n"},"routes/__docs-pages":null},"actionData":null,"errors":null},"future":{"v2_dev":true,"unstable_postcss":false,"unstable_tailwind":false,"v2_errorBoundary":false,"v2_headers":false,"v2_meta":true,"v2_normalizeFormMethod":true,"v2_routeConvention":false}};</script><script nonce="kfJ0INexYSQgHq26M5MCWfAvuUcQePwayqIMxxoAUjoTy88z" type="module" async="">import "https://www.paypalobjects.com/ppdevdocs/bundles/10.6.8/manifest-2AA28ED2.js";

} var maxRetries = 34, bannerhidden=false; function triggerBanner() { if (isPageReady()) { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } gdprSetup(); } else { if (isBannerClosed() && !bannerhidden ) { bannerhidden=hideBanner(); } if (maxRetries-- > 0) { setTimeout(triggerBanner, 150); } else { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(!isBannerClosed() && document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner') && !document.body.className.includes("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll")){ document.body.className = document.body.className += " ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"; if(undefined){ adjustPaddingTop(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop);   document.body.className = document.body.className += " top-cookie-banner-enabled"; } } var acceptAllButton = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var bannerDeclineButton = document.getElementById('bannerDeclineButton'); var bannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('bannerCloseButton'); var usBannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('usBannerCloseButton'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if ( acceptAllButton ) { acceptAllButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('accept')); }; } if ( bannerDeclineButton ) { bannerDeclineButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('decline')); }; } if ( usBannerCloseButton ) { usBannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('close')); }; } if ( bannerCloseButton ) { bannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); setSessionStorage('isBannerClosed'); } } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } } } } triggerBanner(); })();</script></div></body></html>
